1) pursuant to Section 80(1)(B) of The Sex Act Work Act 1994, the land at 34 Station Street Moorabbin (Land) is being used for the purpose of the operation of a Brothel or has been so used and there has not been granted nor is in force any Permit Under the Planning and Environment Act 1987 for the use of the land for that purpose.

Further Order:

2) The Land is Declared to be a Proscribed Brothel For 12 Months
3) The Respondent pay the Applicant's Costs Fixed at $2600
4) The Respondent's Description in the Court Documents be Amended to Dung Phung Nguyen

                                                                                           SJ Lee Magistrate
